<p>Deverbal noun derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздохнуть.html>вздохну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzdoxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздох.html>вздох</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzdox</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздох.html>вздо́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздох.html>вздо́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздох.html>вздо́хов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sigh <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a deep and prolonged audible inspiration or respiration of air, as when fatigued, frustrated, or grieved; the act of sighing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>breath, breathing in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́днего</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вздох.html>вздо́ха</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do poslédnevo <b>vzdóxa</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to the last breath, to the death</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздрогнуть.html>вздро́гнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzdrógnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздрагивать.html>вздра́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzdrágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздрогнуть.html>вздро́гнуть</a></b>)

***вздумать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздумать.html>взду́мать</a> (6403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dúmatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздумать.html>взду́мать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzdúmatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to decide <i>(to)</i>, to take it into one's head
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вздумать.html>взду́мали</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što éto vy <b>vzdúmali</b> uxodítʹ?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what makes you go?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вздумать.html>взду́мал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>vzdúmal</b> navestítʹ drúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I just decided to visit a friend</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздумать.html>взду́май</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne vzdumaj(te)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't take it into your head; don't even think (of )</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздуматься.html>взду́маться</a> (18402)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздумать.html>взду́мать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzdúmatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздуматься.html>взду́маться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzdúmatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вздуматься.html>взду́малось</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>vzdúmalosʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he took it into his head; he just decided</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вздуматься.html>взду́малось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:погулять.html>погуля́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>vzdúmalosʹ</b> poguljátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I just decided to take a walk</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>хожу́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вздуматься.html>взду́мается</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja xožú, gde (mne) <b>vzdúmajetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I walk where I want / choose</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздуматься.html>взду́мается</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak vzdúmajetsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) at one's own sweet will; 2) anyhow; without order; unsystematically</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to enter someone's head, to come to someone's mind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вздуматься.html>взду́мается</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on govorít to, što jemú <b>vzdúmajetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he says/speaks whatever comes to his mind</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздыбить.html>взды́бить</a> (21089)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дыба.html>дыбы́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dybý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздыбить.html>взды́бить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzdýbitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взды́бливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cause (a horse, etc.) to rear up</li>
<li>to cause (hair, etc.) to stand on end</li></ol>

***вздымать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздымать.html>вздыма́ть</a> (18527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">въздымати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭzdymati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Usually explained from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъzdymati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blow up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dymati</i>, iterative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dǫti</i>. It is better viewed as a result of rebracketing of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подымать.html>подыма́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podymátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as <i><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i>-<i>дыма́ть</i>, at least in the modern sense.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздымать.html>вздыма́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzdymátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to raise</li></ol>

***вздыхать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздыхать.html>вздыха́ть</a> (3398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ды́хать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dýxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздыхать.html>вздыха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzdyxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздохнуть.html>вздохну́ть</a></b>)

<li>to long (for), to sigh (for), to pine (after, for), to yearn (after, for)</li></ol>

***взимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взимать.html>взима́ть</a> (27914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взимать.html>взима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to collect, to levy, to take monies <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in forms of taxes, payments, duties, tariffs, and fines</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***взирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взирать.html>взира́ть</a> (11095)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-зира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-zirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with reduction of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*взз-</span> to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вз-</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́ть</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воззвать.html>воззва́ть</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozzvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взирать.html>взира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">воззре́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look <i>(at)</i>, to gaze <i>(at)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взирать.html>взира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:свысока.html>свысока́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzirátʹ</b> na kovó-libo svysoká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to look down on somebody</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***взламывавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взламывавший.html>взла́мывавший</a> (28386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взламывавший.html>взла́мывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzlámyvavšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взламывать.html>взла́мывать</a> (28386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взломать.html>взлома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzlomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взламывать.html>взла́мывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzlámyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взломать.html>взлома́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break open, to force, to burst in, to break <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взламывать.html>взла́мывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzlámyvatʹ</b> zamok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to force a lock</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(program)</i> to crack</li></ol>
